# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes sig-node Kubelet Component Ownership Map

## Your Task

Map the major kubelet components in kubernetes/kubernetes owned by sig-node. Find the Go source files that implement: the pod lifecycle manager, the container runtime interface (CRI) client, the volume manager, and the device plugin manager.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [

  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

48-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed the mapping of the major kubelet components owned by sig-node. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with a comprehensive mapping of the four major kubelet components:

### 1. **Pod Lifecycle Manager**
- **Pod Manager** (`pkg/kubelet/pod/pod_manager.go`): Manages pod state and tracks static/mirror pod mappings
- **Pod Workers** (`pkg/kubelet/pod_workers.go`): Handles pod synchronization lifecycle
- **Lifecycle Handlers** (`pkg/kubelet/lifecycle/handlers.go`): Executes container lifecycle hooks

### 2. **Container Runtime Interface (CRI) Client**
- **KubeRuntime Manager** (`pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go`): The `kubeGenericRuntimeManager` struct that manages all container lifecycle operations and communicates with container runtimes via gRPC

### 3. **Volume Manager**
- **Volume Manager** (`pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/volume_manager.go`): Orchestrates volume attachment/detachment and mount/unmount operations
- **Desired State of World Populator** (`pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/populator/desired_state_of_world_populator.go`): Tracks required volumes
- **Reconciler** (`pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/reconciler/reconciler_common.go`): Maintains consistency between desired and actual states

### 4. **Device Plugin Manager**
- **Plugin Manager** (`pkg/kubelet/pluginmanager/plugin_manager.go`): Manages device plugin registration and lifecycle using the desired/actual state pattern

All components are orchestrated by the main `Kubelet` struct in `pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go`.

Pods from non-apiserver sources are called static pods, and API\\n35: // server is not aware of the existence of static pods. In order to monitor\\n36: // the status of such pods, the kubelet creates a mirror pod for each static\\n37: // pod via the API server.\\n38: //\\n39: // A mirror pod has the same pod full name (name and namespace) as its static\\n40: // counterpart (albeit different metadata such as UID, etc). By leveraging the\\n41: // fact that the kubelet reports the pod status using the pod full name, the\\n42: // status of the mirror pod always reflects the actual status of the static\\n43: // pod. When a static pod gets deleted, the associated orphaned mirror pod\\n44: // will also be removed.\\n45: type Manager interface {\\n46: \\t// GetPodByFullName returns the (non-mirror) pod that matches full name, as well as\\n47: \\t// whether the pod was found.\\n48: \\tGetPodByFullName(podFullName string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n49: \\t// GetPodByName provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches namespace and\\n50: \\t// name, as well as whether the pod was found.\\n51: \\tGetPodByName(namespace, name string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n52: \\t// GetPodByUID provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches pod UID, as well as\\n53: \\t// whether the pod is found.\\n54: \\tGetPodByUID(types.UID) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n55: \\t// GetPodByMirrorPod returns the static pod for the given mirror pod and\\n56: \\t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\\n57: \\tGetPodByMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n58: \\t// GetMirrorPodByPod returns the mirror pod for the given static pod and\\n59: \\t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\\n60: \\tGetMirrorPodByPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\\n61: \\t// GetPodAndMirrorPod returns the complement for a pod - if a pod was provided\\n62: \\t// and a mirror pod can be found, return it. If a mirror pod is provided and\\n63: \\t// the pod can be found, return it and true for wasMirror.\\n64: \\tGetPodAndMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (pod, mirrorPod *v1.Pod, wasMirror bool)\\n65: \\n66: \\t// GetPods returns the regular pods bound to the kubelet and their spec.\\n67: \\tGetPods() []*v1.Pod\\n68: \\n69: \\t// GetPodsAndMirrorPods returns the set of pods, the set of mirror pods, and\\n70: \\t// the pod fullnames of any orphaned mirror pods.\\n71: \\tGetPodsAndMirrorPods() (allPods []*v1.Pod, allMirrorPods []*v1.Pod, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames []string)\\n72: \\n73: \\t// GetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap return a map of static pod to its corresponding\\n74: \\t// mirror pods. It is possible that there is no mirror pod for a static pod\\n75: \\t// if kubelet is running in standalone mode or is in the process of creating\\n76: \\t// the mirror pod and in that case, the mirror pod is nil.\\n77: \\tGetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap() map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod\\n78: \\n79: \\t// SetPods replaces the internal pods with the new pods.\\n80: \\t// It is currently only used for testing.\\n81: \\tSetPods(pods []*v1.Pod)\\n82: \\t// AddPod adds the given pod to the manager.\\n83: \\tAddPod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n84: \\t// UpdatePod updates the given pod in the manager.\\n85: \\tUpdatePod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n86: \\t// RemovePod deletes the given pod from the manager.  For mirror pods,\\n87: \\t// this means deleting the mappings related to mirror pods.  For non-\\n88: \\t// mirror pods, this means deleting from indexes for all non-mirror pods.\\n89: \\tRemovePod(pod *v1.Pod)\\n90: \\n91: \\t// TranslatePodUID returns the actual UID of a pod. If the UID belongs to\\n92: \\t// a mirror pod, returns the UID of its static pod. Otherwise, returns the\\n93: \\t// original UID.\\n94: \\t//\\n95: \\t// All public-facing functions should perform this translation for UIDs\\n96: \\t// because user may provide a mirror pod UID, which is not recognized by\\n97: \\t// internal Kubelet functions.\\n98: \\tTranslatePodUID(uid types.UID) kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID\\n99: \\t// GetUIDTranslations returns the mappings of static pod }\\n155: \\n156: // updateMetrics updates the metrics surfaced by the pod manager.\\n157: // oldPod or newPod may be nil to signify creation or deletion.\\n158: func updateMetrics(oldPod, newPod *v1.Pod) {\\n159: \\tvar numEC int\\n160: \\tif oldPod != nil {\\n161: \\t\\tnumEC -= len(oldPod.Spec.EphemeralContainers)\\n162: \\t}\\n163: \\tif newPod != nil {\\n164: \\t\\tnumEC +=     "content": "1: /*\n2: Copyright 2015 The Kubernetes Authors.\n3: \n4: Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the \"License\");\n5: you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.\n6: You may obtain a copy of the License at\n7: \n8:     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n9: \n10: Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n11: distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n12: WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n13: See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n14: limitations under the License.\n15: */\n16: \n17: //go:generate mockery\n18: package pod\n19: \n20: import (\n21: \t\"sync\"\n22: \n23: \tv1 \"k8s.io/api/core/v1\"\n24: \t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types\"\n25: \tkubecontainer \"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/container\"\n26: \t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/metrics\"\n27: \tkubetypes \"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/kubelet/types\"\n28: )\n29: \n30: // Manager stores and manages access to pods, maintaining the mappings\n31: // between static pods and mirror pods.\n32: //\n33: // The kubelet discovers pod updates from 3 sources: file, http, and\n34: // apiserver. Pods from non-apiserver sources are called static pods, and API\n35: // server is not aware of the existence of static pods. In order to monitor\n36: // the status of such pods, the kubelet creates a mirror pod for each static\n37: // pod via the API server.\n38: //\n39: // A mirror pod has the same pod full name (name and namespace) as its static\n40: // counterpart (albeit different metadata such as UID, etc). By leveraging the\n41: // fact that the kubelet reports the pod status using the pod full name, the\n42: // status of the mirror pod always reflects the actual status of the static\n43: // pod. When a static pod gets deleted, the associated orphaned mirror pod\n44: // will also be removed.\n45: type Manager interface {\n46: \t// GetPodByFullName returns the (non-mirror) pod that matches full name, as well as\n47: \t// whether the pod was found.\n48: \tGetPodByFullName(podFullName string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n49: \t// GetPodByName provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches namespace and\n50: \t// name, as well as whether the pod was found.\n51: \tGetPodByName(namespace, name string) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n52: \t// GetPodByUID provides the (non-mirror) pod that matches pod UID, as well as\n53: \t// whether the pod is found.\n54: \tGetPodByUID(types.UID) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n55: \t// GetPodByMirrorPod returns the static pod for the given mirror pod and\n56: \t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\n57: \tGetPodByMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n58: \t// GetMirrorPodByPod returns the mirror pod for the given static pod and\n59: \t// whether it was known to the pod manager.\n60: \tGetMirrorPodByPod(*v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool)\n61: \t// GetPodAndMirrorPod returns the complement for a pod - if a pod was provided\n62: \t// and a mirror pod can be found, return it. If a mirror pod is provided and\n63: \t// the pod can be found, return it and true for wasMirror.\n64: \tGetPodAndMirrorPod(*v1.Pod) (pod, mirrorPod *v1.Pod, wasMirror bool)\n65: \n66: \t// GetPods returns the regular pods bound to the kubelet and their spec.\n67: \tGetPods() []*v1.Pod\n68: \n69: \t// GetPodsAndMirrorPods returns the set of pods, the set of mirror pods, and\n70: \t// the pod fullnames of any orphaned mirror pods.\n71: \tGetPodsAndMirrorPods() (allPods []*v1.Pod, allMirrorPods []*v1.Pod, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames []string)\n72: \n73: \t// GetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap return a map of static pod to its corresponding\n74: \t// mirror pods. It is possible that there is no mirror pod for a static pod\n75: \t// if kubelet is running in standalone mode or is in the process of creating\n76: \t// the mirror pod and in that case, the mirror pod is nil.\n77: \tGetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap() map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod\n78: \n79: \t// SetPods replaces the internal pods with the new pods.\n80: \t// It is currently only used for testing.\n81: \tSetPods(pods []*v1.Pod)\n82: \t// AddPod adds the given pod to the manager.\n83: \tAddPod(pod *v1.Pod)\n84: \t// UpdatePod updates the given pod in the manager.\n85: \tUpdatePod(pod *v1.Pod)\n86: \t// RemovePod deletes the given pod from the manager.  For mirror pods,\n87: \t// this means deleting the mappings related to mirror pods.  For non-\n88: \t// mirror pods, this means deleting from indexes for all non-mirror pods.\n89: \tRemovePod(pod *v1.Pod)\n90: \n91: \t// TranslatePodUID returns the actual UID of a pod. If the UID belongs to\n92: \t// a mirror pod, returns the UID of its static pod. Otherwise, returns the\n93: \t// original UID.\n94: \t//\n95: \t// All public-facing functions should perform this translation for UIDs\n96: \t// because user may provide a mirror pod UID, which is not recognized by\n97: \t// internal Kubelet functions.\n98: \tTranslatePodUID(uid types.UID) kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID\n99: \t// GetUIDTranslations returns the mappings of static pod UIDs to mirror pod\n100: \t// UIDs and mirror pod UIDs to static pod UIDs.\n101: \tGetUIDTranslations() (podToMirror map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]kubetypes.MirrorPodUID, mirrorToPod map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID)\n102: }\n103: \n104: // basicManager is a functional Manager.\n105: //\n106: // All fields in basicManager are read-only and are updated calling SetPods,\n107: // AddPod, UpdatePod, or RemovePod.\n108: type basicManager struct {\n109: \t// Protects all internal maps.\n110: \tlock sync.RWMutex\n111: \n112: \t// Regular pods indexed by UID.\n113: \tpodByUID map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]*v1.Pod\n114: \t// Mirror pods indexed by UID.\n115: \tmirrorPodByUID map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]*v1.Pod\n116: \n117: \t// Pods indexed by full name newPod may be nil to signify creation or deletion.\n158: func updateMetrics(oldPod, newPod *v1.Pod) {\n159: \tvar numEC int\n160: \tif oldPod != nil {\n161: \t\tnumEC -= various indices. The caller is assumed to hold the\n173: // lock.\n174: func (pm *basicManager) updatePodsInternal(pods ...*v1.Pod) {\n175: \tfor _, pod := range pods {\n176: \t\tpodFullName := kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(pod)\n177: \t\t// This logic relies on a static pod and its mirror to have the same name.\n178: \t\t// It is safe to type convert here due to the IsMirrorPod guard.\n179: \t\tif kubetypes.IsMirrorPod(pod) {\n180: \t\t\tmirrorPodUID := kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(pod.UID)\n181: \t\t\tpm.mirrorPodByUID[mirrorPodUID] = pod\n182: \t\t\tpm.mirrorPodByFullName[podFullName] = pod\n183: \t\t\tif p, ok := pm.podByFullName[podFullName]; ok {\n184: \t\t\t\tpm.translationByUID[mirrorPodUID] = kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(p.UID)\n185: \t\t\t}\n186: \t\t} else {\n187: \t\t\tresolvedPodUID := kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(pod.UID)\n188: \t\t\tupdateMetrics(pm.podByUID[resolvedPodUID], pod)\n189: \t\t\tpm.podByUID[resolvedPodUID] = pod\n190: \t\t\tpm.podByFullName[podFullName] = pod\n191: \t\t\tif mirror, ok := pm.mirrorPodByFullName[podFullName]; ok {\n192: \t\t\t\tpm.translationByUID[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(mirror.UID)] = resolvedPodUID\n193: \t\t\t}\n194: \t\t}\n195: \t}\n196: }\n197: \n198: func (pm *basicManager) RemovePod(pod *v1.Pod) {\n199: \tupdateMetrics(pod, nil)\n200: \tpm.lock.Lock()\n201: \tdefer pm.lock.Unlock()\n202: \tpodFullName := kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(pod)\n203: \t// It is safe to type convert here due to the IsMirrorPod guard.\n204: \tif kubetypes.IsMirrorPod(pod) {\n205: \t\tmirrorPodUID := kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(pod.UID)\n206: \t\tdelete(pm.mirrorPodByUID, mirrorPodUID)\n207: \t\tdelete(pm.mirrorPodByFullName, podFullName)\n208: \t\tdelete(pm.translationByUID, mirrorPodUID)\n209: \t} else {\n210: \t\tdelete(pm.podByUID, kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(pod.UID))\n211: \t\tdelete(pm.podByFullName, podFullName)\n212: \t}\n213: }\n214: \n215: func (pm *basicManager) GetPods() []*v1.Pod {\n216: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n217: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n218: \treturn podsMapToPods(pm.podByUID)\n219: }\n220: \n221: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodsAndMirrorPods() (allPods []*v1.Pod, allMirrorPods []*v1.Pod, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames []string) {\n222: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n223: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n224: \tallPods = podsMapToPods(pm.podByUID)\n225: \tallMirrorPods = mirrorPodsMapToMirrorPods(pm.mirrorPodByUID)\n226: \n227: \tfor podFullName := range pm.mirrorPodByFullName {\n228: \t\tif _, ok := pm.podByFullName[podFullName]; !ok {\n229: \t\t\torphanedMirrorPodFullnames = append(orphanedMirrorPodFullnames, podFullName)\n230: \t\t}\n231: \t}\n232: \treturn allPods, allMirrorPods, orphanedMirrorPodFullnames\n233: }\n234: \n235: func (pm *basicManager) GetStaticPodToMirrorPodMap() map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod {\n236: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n237: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n238: \tstaticPodsMapToMirrorPods := make(map[*v1.Pod]*v1.Pod)\n239: \tfor _, pod := range podsMapToPods(pm.podByUID) {\n240: \t\tif kubetypes.IsStaticPod(pod) {\n241: \t\t\tstaticPodsMapToMirrorPods[pod] = pm.mirrorPodByFullName[kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(pod)]\n242: \t\t}\n243: \t}\n244: \treturn staticPodsMapToMirrorPods\n245: }\n246: \n247: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodByUID(uid types.UID) (*v1.Pod, bool) {\n248: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n249: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n250: \tpod, ok := pm.podByUID[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(uid)] // Safe conversion, map only holds non-mirrors.\n251: \treturn pod, ok\n252: }\n253: \n254: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodByName(namespace, name string) (*v1.Pod, bool) {\n255: \tpodFullName := kubecontainer.BuildPodFullName(name, namespace)\n256: \treturn pm.GetPodByFullName(podFullName)\n257: }\n258: \n259: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodByFullName(podFullName string) (*v1.Pod, bool) {\n260: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n261: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n262: \tpod, ok := pm.podByFullName[podFullName]\n263: \treturn pod, ok\n264: }\n265: \n266: func (pm *basicManager) TranslatePodUID(uid types.UID) kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID {\n267: \t// It is safe to type convert to a resolved UID because type conversion is idempotent.\n268: \tif uid == \"\" {\n269: \t\treturn kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(uid)\n270: \t}\n271: \n272: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n273: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n274: \tif translated, ok := pm.translationByUID[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID(uid)]; ok {\n275: \t\treturn translated\n276: \t}\n277: \treturn kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID(uid)\n278: }\n279: \n280: func (pm *basicManager) GetUIDTranslations() (podToMirror map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]kubetypes.MirrorPodUID,\n281: \tmirrorToPod map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID) {\n282: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n283: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n284: \n285: \tpodToMirror = make(map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]kubetypes.MirrorPodUID, len(pm.translationByUID))\n286: \tmirrorToPod = make(map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID, len(pm.translationByUID))\n287: \t// Insert empty translation mapping for all static pods.\n288: \tfor uid, pod := range pm.podByUID {\n289: \t\tif !kubetypes.IsStaticPod(pod) {\n290: \t\t\tcontinue\n291: \t\t}\n292: \t\tpodToMirror[uid] = \"\"\n293: \t}\n294: \t// Fill in translations. Notice that if there is no mirror pod for a\n295: \t// static pod, its uid will be translated into empty string \"\". This\n296: \t// is WAI, from the caller side we can know that the static pod doesn't\n297: \t// have a corresponding mirror pod instead of using static pod uid directly.\n298: \tfor k, v := range pm.translationByUID {\n299: \t\tmirrorToPod[k] = v\n300: \t\tpodToMirror[v] = k\n301: \t}\n302: \treturn podToMirror, mirrorToPod\n303: }\n304: \n305: // IsMirrorPodOf returns true if pod and mirrorPod are associated with each other.\n306: func IsMirrorPodOf(mirrorPod, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n307: \t// Check name and namespace first.\n308: \tif pod.Name != mirrorPod.Name || pod.Namespace != mirrorPod.Namespace {\n309: \t\treturn false\n310: \t}\n311: \thash, ok := getHashFromMirrorPod(mirrorPod)\n312: \tif !ok {\n313: \t\treturn false\n314: \t}\n315: \treturn hash == getPodHash(pod)\n316: }\n317: \n318: func podsMapToPods(UIDMap map[kubetypes.ResolvedPodUID]*v1.Pod) []*v1.Pod {\n319: \tpods := make([]*v1.Pod, 0, len(UIDMap))\n320: \tfor _, pod := range UIDMap {\n321: \t\tpods = append(pods, pod)\n322: \t}\n323: \treturn pods\n324: }\n325: \n326: func mirrorPodsMapToMirrorPods(UIDMap map[kubetypes.MirrorPodUID]*v1.Pod) []*v1.Pod {\n327: \tpods := make([]*v1.Pod, 0, len(UIDMap))\n328: \tfor _, pod := range UIDMap {\n329: \t\tpods = append(pods, pod)\n330: \t}\n331: \treturn pods\n332: }\n333: \n334: func (pm *basicManager) GetMirrorPodByPod(pod *v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool) {\n335: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n336: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n337: \tmirrorPod, ok := pm.mirrorPodByFullName[kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(pod)]\n338: \treturn mirrorPod, ok\n339: }\n340: \n341: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodByMirrorPod(mirrorPod *v1.Pod) (*v1.Pod, bool) {\n342: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n343: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n344: \tpod, ok := pm.podByFullName[kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(mirrorPod)]\n345: \treturn pod, ok\n346: }\n347: \n348: func (pm *basicManager) GetPodAndMirrorPod(aPod *v1.Pod) (pod, mirrorPod *v1.Pod, wasMirror bool) {\n349: \tpm.lock.RLock()\n350: \tdefer pm.lock.RUnlock()\n351: \n352: \tfullName := kubecontainer.GetPodFullName(aPod)\n353: \tif kubetypes.IsMirrorPod(aPod) {\n354: \t\treturn
